| 1:15:03| A 100th birthday is just one of the small ones.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4503)|
| 1:15:06| But we do have a resolution, and if it could be read into the record, Mr. Chairman.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4506)|
| 1:15:13| Go ahead, Madam Clerk.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4513)|
| 1:15:15| Whereas on May 7, 2013, Mabel Wolfe Acuff celebrated her 100th birthday,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4515)|
| 1:15:20| and whereas having been born in Union County, Tennessee,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4520)|
| 1:15:23| Mabel moved to Knoxville at an early age and lived with her family on the farm that Mabel still owns today,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4523)|
| 1:15:28| and whereas Mabel's father, Jim Wolfe, was a farmer and worked for the railroad,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4528)|
| 1:15:32| and her mother, Cora, was a teacher and earned a teaching certificate at the University of Tennessee,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4532)|
| 1:15:37| and whereas Mabel attended Milligan College on a scholarship for two years| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4537)|
| 1:15:41| before transferring to the University of Tennessee and thereafter earning a Bachelor of Science degree in 1934,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4541)|
| 1:15:48| and whereas upon her college graduation, Mabel embarked upon her career as a lifelong teacher,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4548)|
| 1:15:53| following in her mother's footsteps,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4553)|
| 1:15:55| and whereas Mabel's first teaching job was at John Sevier School, where she taught third grade through high school,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4555)|
| 1:16:01| and whereas after three years, Mabel went to Coryton| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4561)|
| 1:16:04| and taught the third and fourth grades for two years before moving to Gibbs| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4564)|
| 1:16:08| and teaching those same students again in high school,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4568)|
| 1:16:11| whereas Mabel remained at Gibbs until she retired in 1978 after a remarkable 43 years of service| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4571)|
| 1:16:18| and education in Knox County,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4578)|
| 1:16:21| and whereas in 1942, Mabel wed the love of her life, Herbert Acuff,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4581)|
| 1:16:25| who later served effectively and commendably at the Knox County Finance Director| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4585)|
| 1:16:30| and unfortunately passed away in 1996,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4590)|
| 1:16:33| and whereas Mabel and Herbert had one son, Gary Acuff,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4593)|
| 1:16:36| who has also served Knox County government until he retired a couple of years ago| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4596)|
| 1:16:41| from his position as the Finance Director for the Knox County Health Department,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4601)|
| 1:16:45| and whereas while serving as Finance Director for Knox County,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4605)|
| 1:16:48| Herbert had the good sense to hire a young lady named Ann Douglas,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4608)|
| 1:16:51| who later became Mabel and Herbert's daughter-in-law| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4611)|
| 1:16:54| and served in the Knox County Finance Department for over 45 years until her recent retirement,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4614)|
| 1:17:00| and whereas Mabel's family has grown over the years| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4620)|
| 1:17:03| with the addition of two grandchildren, Brian and David Acuff,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4623)|
| 1:17:06| and two great-grandchildren, Hannah and Dylan Acuff,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4626)|
| 1:17:09| and whereas Mabel's other interests include traveling, music, and her church.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4629)|
| 1:17:14| In fact, Mabel is still very active in her church as she serves as the assistant pianist,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4634)|
| 1:17:18| teaches an adult Sunday school class, and leads a weekly women's prayer group,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4638)|
| 1:17:24| and whereas even now at 100 years of age,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4644)|
| 1:17:27| Mabel continues to amaze her family, friends, and neighbors| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4647)|
| 1:17:30| with her wondrously active lifestyle,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4650)|
| 1:17:33| and therefore be it resolved by the Commission of Knox County as follows.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4653)|
| 1:17:37| The Commission of Knox County hereby wishes to express its sincere and heartfelt appreciation| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4657)|
| 1:17:42| of Mabel Wolfe Acuff for her lifetime of achievements and service as an educator in Knox County,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoCom130528?start=4662)|
